    \hypertarget{weatherpy}{%
\subsection{\# WeatherPy}\label{weatherpy}}

\hypertarget{analysis}{%
\subsubsection{Analysis}\label{analysis}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  As expected, cities in the latitudes of approximately -20 to 20
  degrees had the highest max temperatures.
\item
  There were no strong relationships that could be observed between
  latitude and humidity. (Oddly, when the analysis was run initially,
  there was one city that had \textgreater{}300\% humidity that may have
  been an error in recording, so added an extra step to remove any
  observation points that had \textgreater{}100\% humidity. When run
  again, there were no outliers but kept the filtering step in the
  code.)
\item
  There were no observable relationships between latitude and
  cloudiness.
\item
  There were no observable relationships between latitude and wind
  speed. There seems to be more cities that have greater than 5 mph wind
  speeds in the northern hemisphere, but this is most likely due to the
  fact that there are more cities in the northern hemisphere, and not an
  indication of a relationship between latitude and wind speeds.
\end{itemize}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{\linethickness}\end{center}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

    \hypertarget{generate-cities-list}{%
\subsection{Generate Cities List}\label{generate-cities-list}}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}2}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} List for holding lat\PYZus{}lngs and cities}
        \PY{n}{lat\PYZus{}lngs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{cities} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create a set of random lat and lng combinations}
        \PY{n}{lats} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{uniform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{low}\PY{o}{=}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mf}{90.000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{high}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{90.000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2000}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{lngs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{uniform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{low}\PY{o}{=}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mf}{180.000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{high}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{180.000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2000}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{lat\PYZus{}lngs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{zip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lats}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lngs}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Identify nearest city for each lat, lng combination}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{lat\PYZus{}lng} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{lat\PYZus{}lngs}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{city} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{citipy}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nearest\PYZus{}city}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lat\PYZus{}lng}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lat\PYZus{}lng}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{city\PYZus{}name}
            
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} If the city is unique, then add it to a our cities list}
            \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{city} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cities}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{cities}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{city}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Print the city count to confirm sufficient count}
        \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cities}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{outcolor}Out[{\color{outcolor}2}]:} 740
\end{Verbatim}
            
    \hypertarget{perform-api-calls}{%
\subsubsection{Perform API Calls}\label{perform-api-calls}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Perform a weather check on each city using a series of successive API
  calls.
\item
  Include a print log of each city as it's being processed (with the
  city number and city name).
\end{itemize}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}3}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Created a function that will pull desired data from the weather API}
        \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{check\PYZus{}weather}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{city}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{url} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{http://api.openweathermap.org/data/2.5/weather?}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
            \PY{n}{units} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{metric}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
            \PY{n}{query\PYZus{}url} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}url\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{appid=}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}api\PYZus{}key\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZam{}units=}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}units\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZam{}q=}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}city\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
            \PY{n}{response} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{requests}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query\PYZus{}url}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{response}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{json}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
           
            \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Processing record for }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}city\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query\PYZus{}url}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{City}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{city}\PY{p}{,}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Cloudiness}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{clouds}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{all}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Country}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sys}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{country}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Date}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{dt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Humidity}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{main}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{humidity}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Lat}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{coord}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{lat}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Lng}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{coord}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{lon}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
                    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Max Temp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{out\PYZus{}json}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{main}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{temp\PYZus{}max}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}

                \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
               
            
            \PY{k}{except} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+ne}{KeyError}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+ne}{IndexError}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

                \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}

    \hypertarget{plotting-the-data}{%
\subsubsection{Plotting the Data}\label{plotting-the-data}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Use proper labeling of the plots using plot titles (including date of
  analysis) and axes labels.
\item
  Save the plotted figures as .pngs.
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{latitude-vs.-temperature-plot}{%
\paragraph{Latitude vs.~Temperature
Plot}\label{latitude-vs.-temperature-plot}}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}9}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Generate scatter plot for latitude vs max temp}
        \PY{n}{latitudes} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{city\PYZus{}weather\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Lat}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{maximum\PYZus{}temps} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{city\PYZus{}weather\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Max Temp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{scatter}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{latitudes}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{maximum\PYZus{}temps}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{edgecolor}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{black}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{grid}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{xlabel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Latitude}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
